LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [c1].[Id], [c1].[CoreId], [c1].[CreationTime], [c1].[CreatorUserId], [c1].[DeleterUserId], [c1].[DeletionTime], [c1].[IsDeleted], [c1].[Language], [c1].[LastModificationTime], [c1].[LastModifierUserId], [c1].[Name]
    FROM [CityTranslations] AS [c1]
    WHERE @__ef_filter__p_1 = CAST(1 AS bit) OR [c1].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [t1] ON [t].[Id] = [t1].[CoreId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [c2].[Id], [c2].[CoreId], [c2].[CreationTime], [c2].[CreatorUserId], [c2].[DeleterUserId], [c2].[DeletionTime], [c2].[IsDeleted], [c2].[Language], [c2].[LastModificationTime], [c2].[LastModifierUserId], [c2].[Name]
    FROM [CountryTranslations] AS [c2]
    WHERE @__ef_filter__p_3 = CAST(1 AS bit) OR [c2].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [t2] ON [t0].[Id] = [t2].[CoreId]
ORDER BY [t].[CreationTime] DESC, [t].[Id], [t0].[Id], [t1].[Id]
